 </h4></div><div id="qg-1" class="panel-collapse collapse"><div class="panel-body"><div class="panel-group" id="qg-1-1"><div class="panel panel-default sub-panel"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title"><a data-event="event_DSA_Page_on_click" data-eventaction="FAQs â€“ General Queries" data-eventcategory="DSA page" data-eventlabel="What is ASAP Digital Savings Account" data-sf-ec-immutable="" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#qg-1-1" class="collapsed" href="#gq-1-1-1" onclick="gotoLink(this);">What is ASAP Digital Savings
                                                                Account?</a>
 </h4></div><div id="gq-1-1-1" class="panel-collapse collapse"><div class="panel-body"><p>ASAP Digital Savings Account is the new age digital savings Account offered by Axis Bank. All you need is your Aadhaar, PAN &amp; other basic details. Since this process is completed through
                                                                a Video verification, kindly ensure you are using a camera enabled device.</p></div></div></div><div class="panel panel-default sub-panel"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title"><a data-event="event_DSA_Page_on_click" data-eventaction="FAQs â€“ General Queries" data-eventcategory="DSA page" data-eventlabel="Benefits of ASAP Digital Savings
                                                                Account" data-sf-ec-immutable="" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#qg-1-1" class="collapsed" href="#gq-1-1-2" onclick="gotoLink(this);">Benefits of ASAP Digital
                                                                Savings
                                                                Account.</a>
 </h4></div><div id="gq-1-1-2" class="panel-collapse collapse"><div class="panel-body"><ul class="vcip-listing"><li>No need to visit the Branch -Avail all our 250 + services online</li><li>Begin safe transactions with your debit card, UPI, NEFT, IMPS, and RTGS as soon as you activate your digital Savings Account. </li><li>Receive a virtual debit card loaded with promotions instantly when you open a digital Savings Account.
                                                                </li><li>Following the opening of your digital Savings Account, a physical debit card appropriate for your account type will be sent to your listed address.
                                                                </li><li>Signature Update via Axis Mobile app - Update any time after account opening.</li></ul></div></div></div><div class="panel panel-default sub-panel"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title"><a data-event="event_DSA_Page_on_click" data-eventaction="FAQs â€“ General Queries" data-eventcategory="DSA page" data-eventlabel="Eligibility to open ASAP Digital

                                                                Digital
                                                                Savings Account.</a>
 </h4></div><div id="gq-1-1-3" class="panel-collapse collapse"><div class="panel-body"><p>You can open an ASAP Digital Savings Account as long as,
                                                            </p><ul class="vcip-listing"><li>You are an Indian citizen.</li><li>You have a valid PAN and Aadhaar number.</li><li>You have a valid mobile number linked to your Aadhaar.
                                                                </li><li>You are 18 years of age or above.</li><li>Your Desktop/Laptop or Mobile Device with which you are opening an account has a camera for the Video KYC process.</li><li>You are applying from India.</li></ul></div></div></div><div class="panel panel-default sub-panel"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title"><a data-event="event_DSA_Page_on_click" data-eventaction="FAQs â€“ General Queries" data-eventcategory="DSA page" data-eventlabel="Is it mandatory to share Aadhaar

                                                                Aadhaar
                                                                details to open a ASAP Digital Savings Account?</a>
 </h4></div><div id="gq-1-1-4" class="panel-collapse collapse"><div class="panel-body"><p>You need to voluntarily share your Aadhaar details to open an ASAP Digital Savings Account. In case you do not wish to share your Aadhaar or VID details, you may visit your nearest Axis Bank
                                                                Branch and choose to open a savings account from our range of options.</p></div></div></div><div class="panel panel-default sub-panel"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title"><a data-event="event_DSA_Page_on_click" data-eventaction="FAQs â€“ General Queries" data-eventcategory="DSA page" data-eventlabel="I need to visit a branch after

                                                                after

                                                                Digitally
                                                                Opened Savings Account</a>
 </h4></div><div id="gq-1-1-7" class="panel-collapse collapse"><div class="panel-body"><h5>You need to maintain account variant specific balances as given below:</h5><ul class="vcip-listing"><li>Easy Access Account: Rs.12,000 (Metro/ Urban) + Rs.5,000 (Semi-Urban) + Rs.2,500 (Rural)</li><li>Liberty Savings Account: Rs.25,000(Metro/Urban) or spends of Rs. 25,000/-, Rs. 25,000 (Semi-urban/Rural â€“ AMB or spends of 25,000/-)</li><li>Prestige Savings Account: <a href="https://application.axisbank.co.in/FeesAndChargeMaster/FeesAndCharges.aspx?_ga=2.165148988.2016859521.1669020866-1614710190.1654676755" class="acc-link" target="_blank">Click here</a>
